20/06/2021, 01:05 - +91 6289 047 612: #include <iostream>
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

class Complex
{
private:
    int real, image;

public:
    Complex(int r = 0, int m = 0)
    {
        real = r;
        image = m;
    }

    Complex operator+(Complex const &c2)
    {

        Complex temp;
        temp.real = real + c2.real;
        temp.image = image + c2.image;
        return temp;
    }

    void print()
    {
        cout << real << "+ " << image << "i" << endl;
    }
};

int32_t main()
{
    Complex c1(5, 8);
    Complex c2(4, 5);
    Complex c3;
    c3 = c1 + c2;
    c3.print();
    return 0;
}

16/07/2021, 16:08 - Anindya: there are two examples out there:
case 1:

```cpp
for(int i = 1; i<100; i++){
      // some of constant operations
}
```
iske time complexity bata raha hai O(1)

on the other hand 

```cpp
for(int i = 1; i<n; i++){
      // some of constant operations
}
```
iska O(N) , and that's ok and quite obvious

29/07/2021, 10:13 - +977 986-7788348: #include<stdio.h>

void sort(char name[10][100]);

void main(){
	char name[10][100];
	int i;
	for(i=0;i<10;i++){
		printf("Enter name of student: ");
		gets(name[i]);
	}
	sort(name);
	for(i=0;i<10;i++)
	printf("%s\n",name[i]);
}

void sort(char name[10][100]){
	int i,j,k,l,len1,len2,ch1,ch2;
	char temp[100];
	for(i=0;i<10;i++){
		for(j=i+1;j<10;j++){
			len1 = strlen(name[i]);
			len2 = strlen(name[j]);
			for(k = 0;k<strlen(name[j]);k++){
				ch1 = name[i][k];
				ch2 = name[j][k];
				if(ch1>ch2){
					for(l = 0;l<len1;l++){
						temp[l] = name[i][l];
					}
					
					for(l = 0;l<len2;l++)
					name[i][l] = name[j][l];
					
					for(l = 0;l<len1;l++)
					name[j][l] = temp[l];
					
					for(l=len2;l<strlen(name[i]);l++)
					name[i][l] = '\0';
					
					for(l=len1;l<strlen(name[j]);l++)
					name[j][l] = '\0';
					
					break;
				} else if(ch1<ch2){
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
29/07/2021, 10:13 - +977 986-7788348: This long program is exactly same to this program
#include<stdio.h>
#include<string.h>

void sort(char name[10][100]);

void main(){
	char name[10][100];
	int i;
	for(i=0;i<10;i++){
		printf("Enter name of student: ");
		gets(name[i]);
	}
	sort(name);
	for(i=0;i<10;i++)
	printf("%s\n",name[i]);
}

void sort(char name[10][100]){
	int i,j;
	char temp[100];
	for(i=0;i<10;i++){
		for(j=i+1;j<10;j++){
			if(strcmp(name[i],name[j])>0){
				strcpy(temp,name[i]);
				strcpy(name[i],name[j]);
				strcpy(name[j],temp);
			}
		}
	}
}

        cin>>a[i];

    for(int i = 0; i<3;){
        if(a[i]!=a[i+1]){
            count++;
            i += 2;
        }
        else{
            i++;
        }
    }
    cout<<count<<endl;
}

int main() {
	int t;
	cin>>t;
	while(t--){
	    solve();
	}
	return 0;
}

void printarray(int *ptr, int n)
{

void evenoddfunc(int *ptr, int n)
{
    int counter = 0, temp;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        if (ptr[i] % 2 == 0)
        {
            temp = ptr[counter];
            ptr[counter] = ptr[i];
            ptr[i] = temp;
            counter++;
        }
    }
}

int main()
{
    int n;
    printf("ENter the size of the array: ");
    scanf("%d", &n);
    int *ptr;
    ptr = (int *)malloc(n * sizeof(int));
    printf("\nENter the elements of the array: ");
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        scanf("%d", &ptr[i]);
    }

    evenoddfunc(ptr, n);
    printarray(ptr, n);
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

int main()
{
    char *ptr;
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the max limit of characters" << endl;
    cin >> n;
    ptr = new char[n];
    cout << "Enter a string, terminate it by entering #" << endl;
    cin.get(ptr, n, '#');

    char *q;
    q = new char[n];
    int count = 0, i = 0;
    while (ptr[i] != '\0')
    {
        cout << "entered loop\n";
        if (int(ptr[i]) == 32)
        {
        }
        else
        {
            q[count] = ptr[i];
            count++;
        }
        i++;
    }
    q[count] = '\0';
    cout << q;

    delete ptr;
    delete q;
    return 0;
}

30/08/2021, 21:44 - +91 76651 80930: Q3. WAP to enter an integer. Ask the user if he wants to enter another integer. Continue input of integers till user stops.
Display all the integers. Use dynamic memory allocation. [ Hint:  Form link list ].

#include <iostream>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <conio.h>
using namespace std;
struct node
{
    int data;
    struct node *next;
} * p;
void push(int data)
{
    struct node *temp = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
    temp->data = data;
    temp->next = NULL;
    struct node *startTemp;
    startTemp = p;
    while (startTemp->next != NULL)
    {
        startTemp = startTemp->next;
    }
    startTemp->next = temp;
}
int main()
{
    int choice, nodeData;
    cout << "Enter any number\n";
    cin >> nodeData;
    struct node *temp = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
    temp->data = nodeData;
    temp->next = NULL;
    struct node *startTemp;
    startTemp = p;
    while (startTemp->next != NULL)
    {
        startTemp = startTemp->next;
    }
    startTemp->next = temp;
    int c;
    for (c = 1;; ++c)
    {
        cout << "\npress 1 if you want to continue else press 0";
        cin >> choice;
        if (choice != 0)
        {
            cout << "Enter any number\n";
            cin >> nodeData;
            push(nodeData);
        }
        else
            break;
    }
    return 0;
}

#include <stdlib.h>

struct node 
{
    int info;
    struct node *next;
    struct node *prev;
}*start=NULL;

void create(int data)
{
     struct node *temp, *q;
     int i,n;
    temp = malloc(sizeof(struct node));
    temp->info = data;
    temp->prev = temp->next= NULL;
    q = start;

    if(start == NULL)
    {
        start = temp;
        return;
    }
    else
    {
        q = start;
        while(q->next!=NULL)
        {
            q = q->next;
            q->next = temp;
            temp->prev = q;
            // for(i=0;i<n;i++)
            // temp =malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            // temp->info = data;

    }
}

void display()
{
    struct node *q=start;

    printf("\n[head] <=>");
    // if(start == NULL)
    // {
    //     printf("List is empty");
    // }
    // else
    // {
        // q= start;
        // printf("Data entered on the list are : \n");
        while(q->next!=NULL)
        {
            printf(" %d <=>",q->info);
            q = q->next;
        }
        printf(" %d <=>",q->info);
        printf(" [head]\n");
    // }
}

int main()
{
    int n,i,data;
    printf("Enter the number of nodes ");
    scanf("%d",&n);

    for(i=1;i<=n;i++)
    {
        printf("Enter data %d : ",i);
        scanf("%d",&data);
        create(data);
        
    }
    display();
    return 0;

}

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

struct Stack {
	int top;
	unsigned capacity;
	int* array;
};


struct Stack* createStack(unsigned capacity)
{
	struct Stack* stack = (struct Stack*)malloc(sizeof(struct Stack));
	stack->capacity = capacity;
	stack->top = -1;
	stack->array = (int*)malloc(stack->capacity * sizeof(int));
	return stack;
}


int isFull(struct Stack* stack)
{
	return stack->top == stack->capacity - 1;
}


int isEmpty(struct Stack* stack)
{
	return stack->top == -1;
}


void push(struct Stack* stack, int item)
{
	if (isFull(stack))
		return;
	stack->array[++stack->top] = item;
	printf("%d pushed to stack\n", item);
}


int pop(struct Stack* stack)
{
	if (isEmpty(stack))
		return INT_MIN;
	return stack->array[stack->top--];
}


int peek(struct Stack* stack)
{
	if (isEmpty(stack))
		return INT_MIN;
	return stack->array[stack->top];
}

int main()
{
	struct Stack* stack = createStack(100);

	push(stack, 10);
	push(stack, 20);
	push(stack, 30);
	push(stack, 40);

	printf("%d popped from stack\n", pop(stack));

	return 0;
}

  map<int, int> m;

09/09/2021, 11:25 - K ROHIT: ```long long sumDivisibleByK(vector<int> a, int k) {
  map<int, int> m;
  long long ans = 0;
  for (auto x : a) {
    x %= k;
    if (x < 0)
      x += k;
    int req = (k - x) % k;
    if (req < 0)
      req += k;
    ans += m[req];
    m[x]++;
  }
  return ans;
}```
